TELEMETRY PEAK_CAN_TLM rc_eps_batt_7 BIG_ENDIAN 
	APPEND_ITEM LENGTH 16 UINT "Length of TCP-ized CAN message (always 36/0x24 bytes) " 
 	APPEND_ID_ITEM FIXED_TYPE 16 UINT 128 "Fixed message type for CAN" BIG_ENDIAN
	APPEND_ITEM TAG 64 UINT "NOT USED in current PCAN-Ethernet Gateway DR hardware/software."
	APPEND_ITEM TIMESTAMP_L 32 UINT "Timestamp of the CAN message, in microseconds.  This is the lower 4 bytes of the timestamp."
	APPEND_ITEM TIMESTAMP_H 32 UINT "Timestamp of the CAN message, in microseconds.  This is the upper 4 bytes of the timestamp."
	APPEND_ITEM CHANNEL 8 UINT "NOT USED in current PCAN-Ethernet Gateway DR hardware/software."
	APPEND_ITEM DLC 8 UINT "Date Length Count from the CAN message."
	APPEND_ITEM FLAGS 16 UINT "NOT USED in current PCAN-Ethernet Gateway DR hardware/software."
	APPEND_ITEM CANID_PADDING 1 UINT "Fixed value of 0 - reserved."
	APPEND_ITEM CANID_RTR 1 UINT "RTR value."
	APPEND_ITEM CANID_TYPE 1 UINT "Indicates whether the message is a standard or extended frame."
	APPEND_ID_ITEM CANID_ID 29 UINT 303628890 "The ID (normal or extended) portion of the 'CAN ID' set of headers."
		STATE EXTENDED 1
		STATE STANDARD 0
	APPEND_ITEM rc_eps_batt_7_acc_charge_min 16 UINT "Acumulated charge minimum" BIG_ENDIAN
	APPEND_ITEM rc_eps_batt_7_acc_charge_max 16 UINT "Accumulated charge maximum" BIG_ENDIAN
	APPEND_ITEM rc_eps_batt_7_acc_charge_avg 16 UINT "Accumulated charge avg" BIG_ENDIAN
	APPEND_ITEM PADDING 16 UINT "Padded bits for CAN data"
	ITEM acc_charge_min 0 0 DERIVED
		UNITS milliAmpH mAH
		GENERIC_READ_CONVERSION_START
			packet.read('RC_EPS_BATT_7_ACC_CHARGE_MIN') * 2 ** (2 * ((System.telemetry.value("PEAK_CAN", "RC_EPS_BATT_6", "RC_EPS_BATT_6_CTRL") & 0b00111000) >> 3)) * 17 / 24576
		GENERIC_READ_CONVERSION_END
	ITEM acc_charge_avg 0 0 DERIVED
		UNITS milliAmpH mAH
		GENERIC_READ_CONVERSION_START
			packet.read('RC_EPS_BATT_7_ACC_CHARGE_AVG') * 2 ** (2 * ((System.telemetry.value("PEAK_CAN", "RC_EPS_BATT_6", "RC_EPS_BATT_6_CTRL") & 0b00111000) >> 3)) * 17 / 24576
		GENERIC_READ_CONVERSION_END
	ITEM acc_charge_max 0 0 DERIVED
		UNITS milliAmpH mAH
		GENERIC_READ_CONVERSION_START
			packet.read('RC_EPS_BATT_7_ACC_CHARGE_MAX') * 2 ** (2 * ((System.telemetry.value("PEAK_CAN", "RC_EPS_BATT_6", "RC_EPS_BATT_6_CTRL") & 0b00111000) >> 3)) * 17 / 24576
		GENERIC_READ_CONVERSION_END
	ITEM rc_eps_batt_7_voltage_diff 0 0 DERIVED
		UNITS milliVolts mV
		GENERIC_READ_CONVERSION_START
			(1000 * System.telemetry.value("PEAK_CAN", "RC_EPS_BATT_4", "RC_EPS_BATT_4_VOLTAGE_AVG") - (2 * System.telemetry.value("PEAK_CAN", "RC_EPS_BATT_2", "RC_EPS_BATT_2_NODE_V_AVG")))
		GENERIC_READ_CONVERSION_END
